 What is Flotation, Buoyant force, Density and Meta Center? What is their definition? jivan main inkaa kya mahatv he
 Let's know about all this
 utplavak bal (buoyant force):drav kaa vah gun jiske kaaran vah vastuon par upar kii ore ek bal lagaataa he, use utkshep yaa utplavak bal kehete hai
 This force acts on the center of gravity of the fluid removed by objects, which is called the center of buoyancy
 iskaa adhyayan sarvapratham archemides ne kiya tha
 The principle of Archimedes: When an object is completely or partially immersed in a fluid, its weight reduction is appreciated
 bhaar main yah abhaasi kami vastu dwaara hataae gaye drav ke bhaar ke baraabar hoti he
 Law of Flotation: (i) When floating in a balanced state, the object displaces fluid equal to its weight
 (ii) thos kaa gurutv-centre tathaa hataae gaye drav kaa gurutv-centre donon ek hi urdhvadhar rekha main hone chahie
 Density: Mass / Volume of its s
 I
 The unit is kilogram meter ^ -3
 aapekshik ghanatv (relative density):vastu kaa ghanatv / 4Â°C par pani kaa ghanatvapekshik ghanatv ek anupaat he
 Therefore, it has no unit
 aapekshik ghanatv ko hydrometer se mapa jaataa he
 Seawater has a higher density than normal water, so it is easier to swim in it
 jab barf pani main tairti he, to uske aaytan kaa 1 / 10 bhaag pani ke upar rahata he
 a vessel is filled with water and ice is floating on it; When the ice will melt completely, the water level in the vessel does not increase, remains the same as before
 doodh kii shuddhta dugyamapi (lactometer) se maapi jaati he
 Meta center: The center of gravity of a fluid displaced by a floating object is called buoyancy center
 utplavan-centre se jane vaali urdhv rekha jis bindu par vastu ke gurutv-centre se jane vaali praarambhik urdhv rekha ko katati hai use mit centre kehete hai

 For this, passengers are being given the facility to book tickets through swipe machine
 railway ne is makasad se 10 hajaar point of cell yani swip mashine lagane kaa faisla kiya he
 These machines will be installed at the passenger reservation system and UTS counters
 inke jariye book hone vaale tikat cancil karne ke liye bhi jaruri guidelins jari kii gai hai
 Such tickets will be canceled
 Railway has decided to cancel the train tickets booked through the swipe machines of SBI
 piares or utis tikat ko ofline tareeke se cancil karaayaa ja saktaa he
 The refund amount will go to the account of the person using offline mode
 iske liye rail yatri ko apane credit yaa debit card ke ditels dobaaraa nahin dene honge
 The consumer can visit any PRS or UTS counter to cancel a ticket booked from sbi's swipe machines
 cancil karaae gaye piares tikat par saaf taur par 'electronic rifund' likhaa jayega
 The consumer's money will arrive in the account within 7 days
 IRCTC ko rifund kaa jimmiarsitisi kaa customer care vibhaag tikaton kii rifunding se judi shikayaton se nipatega
 For this, IRCTC has been directed to align with SBI and the concerned zonal railways
 esbiai ke alaava duusari bainkon kii swip mashiinon se jari kiye gaye piares tikaton ke rifund ke liye bhi railway ne nirdesh jari kiye hai
 There were already 75 swipe machines in Indian Railways at different locations across the country before the SBI was awarded the contract for 10,000 swipe machines

 report main kaha gaya ki srilanka main grih yuddh kii samaapti ke baad se aise kisi bhi hamale kaa pataa nahin chalaa he, jiske liye littey ko pramanik rup se jimmedaar tehraaya ja sake, lekin 2014 main malaysia main kul 13 littey samarthakon ko giraftaar kiya gaya tha, jinamein se kai ne kathith rup se america ke khilaaf or bharat main israeli duutavas ke pratishthanon par hamalon kii yojana banaai thi
